
1. Metric: certwatcher_read_certificate_errors_total

    Type: counter

    Help: Total number of certificate read errors

    Label Combinations:

        (none)

2. Metric: certwatcher_read_certificate_total

    Type: counter

    Help: Total number of certificate reads

    Label Combinations:

        (none)

3. Metric: controller_runtime_active_workers

    Type: gauge

    Help: Number of currently used workers per controller

    Label Combinations:

        [controller]

4. Metric: controller_runtime_max_concurrent_reconciles

    Type: gauge

    Help: Maximum number of concurrent reconciles per controller

    Label Combinations:

        [controller]

5. Metric: controller_runtime_reconcile_errors_total

    Type: counter

    Help: Total number of reconciliation errors per controller

    Label Combinations:

        [controller]

6. Metric: controller_runtime_reconcile_time_seconds

    Type: histogram

    Help: Length of time per reconciliation per controller

    Label Combinations:

        [controller] (Note: the le label is specific to histogram buckets and not usually listed as a primary dimension)

7. Metric: controller_runtime_reconcile_total

    Type: counter

    Help: Total number of reconciliations per controller

    Label Combinations:

        [controller, result]

8. Metric: couchbase_operator_build_info

    Type: gauge

    Help: A metric with a constant '1' value labeled by version, revision, branch, goversion from which couchbase_operator was built, and the goos and goarch for the build.

    Label Combinations:

        [branch, goarch, goos, goversion, revision, tags, version]

9. Metric: couchbase_operator_pod_readiness_duration

    Type: histogram

    Help: The time it takes for a pod to enter a ready state

    Label Combinations:

        [name, serverClass] (Note: the le label is specific to histogram buckets)

10. Metric: couchbase_operator_reconcile_failures

* Help: Total failed reconcile operations performed on a specific cluster
* Label Combinations:
* [name, namespace]

* [name, namespace, result]

43. Metric: leader_election_master_status
* Type: gauge
* Help: Gauge of if the reporting system is master of the relevant lease, 0 indicates backup, 1 indicates master. 'name' is the string used to identify the lease. Please make sure to group by name.
* Label Combinations:
* [name]

* Type: counter
* Help: Total number of retries handled by workqueue
* Label Combinations:
* [name]

57. Metric: workqueue_unfinished_work_seconds
* Type: gauge
* Help: How many seconds of work has been done that is in progress and hasn't been observed by work_duration. Large values indicate stuck threads. One can deduce the number of stuck threads by observing the rate at which this increases.
* Label Combinations:
* [name]

58. Metric: workqueue_work_duration_seconds
* Type: histogram
* Help: How long in seconds processing an item from workqueue takes.
* Label Combinations:
* [name] (Note: the le label is specific to histogram buckets)
